I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
Don't apply nested page context handling to standalone .RenderShortcodes
The current tracking of nested page context (typically used for inclusion of content and having any relative links resolve correctly) assume that we're rendering content (either via `Page.Content` or `Page.RenderString`).

This means that the test below fails (the content never gets rendered to HTML, so the wrapper strings gets left behind).

See #12457 for a bigger discussion about this, but one use case for the below would be output format that just outputs ... Markdown.

And we should be able to detect and handle this scenario, as we already do similar checks.

```go

func TestRenderShortcodesStandalone(t *testing.T) {
	t.Parallel()

	files := `
-- hugo.toml --
disableKinds = ['section','rss','sitemap','taxonomy','term']
-- layouts/all.html --
RenderShortcodes: {{ .RenderShortcodes }}|
-- layouts/_shortcodes/headings.html --
## Heading 1
### Heading 2
{{ $p := site.GetPage "includeme" }}
RenderShortcodes2: {{ $p.RenderShortcodes }}|
-- content/p1.md --
title: "p1"
---
{{% headings "headings" %}}
-- content/includeme.md --
---
title: "includeme"
---
## Heading 2
`

	b := Test(t, files)

	b.AssertNoRenderShortcodesArtifacts()
}

```

</pr_description>

   646	func (c *cachedContentScope) contentToC(ctx context.Context) (contentTableOfContents, error) {
   647	        cp := c.pco
   648	        key := c.keyScope(ctx)
   649	        versionv := c.version(cp)

   655	                if err != nil {
   656	                        return nil, err
   657	                }
   658	
   659	                if err := cp.initRenderHooks(); err != nil {
   660	                        return nil, err
   661	                }

   666	                        return nil, err
   667	                }

   781	
   782	                rendered, err := c.contentRendered(ctx)
   783	                if err != nil {
   784	                        return nil, err
   785	                }
   786	
   787	                result.plain = tpl.StripHTML(string(rendered.content))
   788	                result.plainWords = strings.Fields(result.plain)
   789	
   790	                isCJKLanguage := cp.po.p.m.pageConfig.IsCJKLanguage
   791	
   792	                if isCJKLanguage {
   793	                        result.wordCount = 0
   794	                        for _, word := range result.plainWords {
   795	                                runeCount := utf8.RuneCountInString(word)
   796	                                if len(word) == runeCount {
   797	                                        result.wordCount++
   798	                                } else {
   799	                                        result.wordCount += runeCount
   800	                                }
   801	                        }
   802	                } else {
   803	                        result.wordCount = helpers.TotalWords(result.plain)
   804	                }
   805	
   806	                // TODO(bep) is set in a test. Fix that.
   807	                if result.fuzzyWordCount == 0 {
   808	                        result.fuzzyWordCount = (result.wordCount + 100) / 100 * 100
   809	                }
   810	
   811	                if isCJKLanguage {
   812	                        result.readingTime = (result.wordCount + 500) / 501
   813	                } else {
   814	                        result.readingTime = (result.wordCount + 212) / 213
   815	                }
   816	
   817	                rs.Value = result
   818	
   819	                return rs, nil
   820	        })
   821	        if err != nil {
   822	                if herrors.IsTimeoutError(err) {
   823	                        err = fmt.Errorf("timed out rendering the page content. Extend the `timeout` limit in your Hugo config file: %w", err)
   824	                }
   825	                return contentPlainPlainWords{}, err
   826	        }
   827	        return v.Value, nil
   828	}
   829	
   830	type cachedContentScope struct {
   831	        *cachedContent
   832	        pco   *pageContentOutput
   833	        scope string
   834	}
   835	
   836	func (c *cachedContentScope) prepareContext(ctx context.Context) context.Context {
   837	        // A regular page's shortcode etc. may be rendered by e.g. the home page,
   838	        // so we need to track any changes to this content's page.
   839	        ctx = tpl.Context.DependencyManagerScopedProvider.Set(ctx, c.pco.po.p)
   840	
   841	        // The markup scope is recursive, so if already set to a non zero value, preserve that value.
   842	        if s := hugo.GetMarkupScope(ctx); s != "" || s == c.scope {
   843	                return ctx
   844	        }
   845	        return hugo.SetMarkupScope(ctx, c.scope)
   846	}
   847	
   848	func (c *cachedContentScope) Render(ctx context.Context) (page.Content, error) {
   849	        return c, nil
   850	}
   851	
   852	func (c *cachedContentScope) Content(ctx context.Context) (template.HTML, error) {
   853	        ctx = c.prepareContext(ctx)
   854	        cr, err := c.contentRendered(ctx)
   855	        if err != nil {
   856	                return "", err
   857	        }
   858	        return cr.content, nil
   859	}
   860	
   861	func (c *cachedContentScope) ContentWithoutSummary(ctx context.Context) (template.HTML, error) {
   862	        ctx = c.prepareContext(ctx)
   863	        cr, err := c.contentRendered(ctx)
   864	        if err != nil {
   865	                return "", err
   866	        }
   867	        return cr.contentWithoutSummary, nil
   868	}
   869	
   870	func (c *cachedContentScope) Summary(ctx context.Context) (page.Summary, error) {
   871	        ctx = c.prepareContext(ctx)
   872	        rendered, err := c.contentRendered(ctx)
   873	        return rendered.summary, err
   874	}
   875

    38	
    39	// Wrap wraps the given byte slice in a Hugo context that used to determine the correct Page
    40	// in .RenderShortcodes.
    41	func Wrap(b []byte, pid uint64) string {
    42	        buf := bufferpool.GetBuffer()
    43	        defer bufferpool.PutBuffer(buf)
    44	        buf.Write(hugoCtxPrefix)
    45	        buf.WriteString(" pid=")
    46	        buf.WriteString(strconv.FormatUint(pid, 10))
    47	        buf.Write(hugoCtxEndDelim)
    48	        buf.WriteByte('\n')
    49	        buf.Write(b)
    50	        // To make sure that we're able to parse it, make sure it ends with a newline.
    51	        if len(b) > 0 && b[len(b)-1] != '\n' {
    52	                buf.WriteByte('\n')
    53	        }
    54	        buf.Write(hugoCtxPrefix)
    55	        buf.Write(hugoCtxClosingDelim)
    56	        buf.WriteByte('\n')
    57	        return buf.String()
    58	}

    62	// HugoContext is a node that represents a Hugo context.
    63	type HugoContext struct {
    64	        ast.BaseInline
    65	
    66	        Closing bool
    67	
    68	        // Internal page ID. Not persisted.
    69	        Pid uint64
    70	}

    72	// Dump implements Node.Dump.
    73	func (n *HugoContext) Dump(source []byte, level int) {
    74	        m := map[string]string{}
    75	        m["Pid"] = fmt.Sprintf("%v", n.Pid)
    76	        ast.DumpHelper(n, source, level, m, nil)
    77	}
    78	
    79	func (n *HugoContext) parseAttrs(attrBytes []byte) {
    80	        keyPairs := bytes.SplitSeq(attrBytes, []byte(" "))
    81	        for keyPair := range keyPairs {
    82	                kv := bytes.Split(keyPair, []byte("="))
    83	                if len(kv) != 2 {
    84	                        continue
    85	                }
    86	                key := string(kv[0])
    87	                val := string(kv[1])
    88	                switch key {
    89	                case "pid":
    90	                        pid, _ := strconv.ParseUint(val, 10, 64)
    91	                        n.Pid = pid
    92	                }
    93	        }
    94	}
    95	
    96	func (h *HugoContext) Kind() ast.NodeKind {
    97	        return kindHugoContext
    98	}
    99	
   100	var (
   101	        hugoCtxPrefix       = []byte("{{__hugo_ctx")
   102	        hugoCtxEndDelim     = []byte("}}")
   103	        hugoCtxClosingDelim = []byte("/}}")
   104	        hugoCtxRe           = regexp.MustCompile(`{{__hugo_ctx( pid=\d+)?/?}}\n?`)
   105	)
   106	
   107	var _ parser.InlineParser = (*hugoContextParser)(nil)
   108	
   109	type hugoContextParser struct{}
   110	
   111	func (a *hugoContextParser) Trigger() []byte {
   112	        return []byte{'{'}
   113	}
   114	
   115	func (s *hugoContextParser) Parse(parent ast.Node, reader text.Reader, pc parser.Context) ast.Node {
   116	        line, _ := reader.PeekLine()
   117	        if !bytes.HasPrefix(line, hugoCtxPrefix) {
   118	                return nil
   119	        }
   120	        end := bytes.Index(line, hugoCtxEndDelim)
   121	        if end == -1 {
   122	                return nil
   123	        }
   124	
   125	        reader.Advance(end + len(hugoCtxEndDelim) + 1) // +1 for the newline
   126	
   127	        if line[end-1] == '/' {
   128	                return &HugoContext{Closing: true}
   129	        }
   130	
   131	        attrBytes := line[len(hugoCtxPrefix)+1 : end]
   132	        h := &HugoContext{}
   133	        h.parseAttrs(attrBytes)
   134	        return h
   135	}

   137	type hugoContextRenderer struct {
   138	        logger loggers.Logger
   139	        html.Config

   141	
   142	func (r *hugoContextRenderer) SetOption(name renderer.OptionName, value any) {
   143	        r.Config.SetOption(name, value)

   145	
   146	func (r *hugoContextRenderer) RegisterFuncs(reg renderer.NodeRendererFuncRegisterer) {
   147	        reg.Register(kindHugoContext, r.handleHugoContext)
   148	        reg.Register(ast.KindRawHTML, r.renderRawHTML)
   149	        reg.Register(ast.KindHTMLBlock, r.renderHTMLBlock)
   150	}
   151	
   152	func (r *hugoContextRenderer) stripHugoCtx(b []byte) ([]byte, bool) {
   153	        if !bytes.Contains(b, hugoCtxPrefix) {
   154	                return b, false
   155	        }
   156	        return hugoCtxRe.ReplaceAll(b, nil), true
   157	}
   158	
   159	func (r *hugoContextRenderer) logRawHTMLEmittedWarn(w util.BufWriter) {
   160	        r.logger.Warnidf(constants.WarnGoldmarkRawHTML, "Raw HTML omitted while rendering %q; see https://gohugo.io/getting-started/configuration-markup/#rendererunsafe", r.getPage(w))
   161	}
   162	
   163	func (r *hugoContextRenderer) getPage(w util.BufWriter) any {
   164	        var p any
   165	        ctx, ok := w.(*render.Context)
   166	        if ok {
   167	                p, _ = render.GetPageAndPageInner(ctx)
   168	        }
   169	        return p
   170	}

   172	func (r *hugoContextRenderer) isHTMLComment(b []byte) bool {
   173	        return len(b) > 4 && b[0] == '<' && b[1] == '!' && b[2] == '-' && b[3] == '-'
   174	}
   175	
   176	// HTML rendering based on Goldmark implementation.
   177	func (r *hugoContextRenderer) renderHTMLBlock(
   178	        w util.BufWriter, source []byte, node ast.Node, entering bool,
   179	) (ast.WalkStatus, error) {
   180	        n := node.(*ast.HTMLBlock)
   181	
   182	        if entering {
   183	                if r.Unsafe {
   184	                        l := n.Lines().Len()
   185	                        for i := range l {
   186	                                line := n.Lines().At(i)
   187	                                linev := line.Value(source)
   188	                                var stripped bool
   189	                                linev, stripped = r.stripHugoCtx(linev)
   190	                                if stripped {
   191	                                        r.logger.Warnidf(constants.WarnRenderShortcodesInHTML, ".RenderShortcodes detected inside HTML block in %q; this may not be what you intended, see https://gohugo.io/methods/page/rendershortcodes/#limitations", r.getPage(w))
   192	                                }
   193	                                r.Writer.SecureWrite(w, linev)
   194	                        }
   195	                } else {
   196	                        l := n.Lines().At(0)
   197	                        v := l.Value(source)
   198	                        if !r.isHTMLComment(v) {
   199	                                r.logRawHTMLEmittedWarn(w)
   200	                                _, _ = w.WriteString("<!-- raw HTML omitted -->\n")
   201	                        }
   202	                }
   203	        } else {
   204	                if n.HasClosure() {
   205	                        if r.Unsafe {
   206	                                closure := n.ClosureLine
   207	                                r.Writer.SecureWrite(w, closure.Value(source))
   208	                        } else {
   209	                                l := n.Lines().At(0)
   210	                                v := l.Value(source)
   211	                                if !r.isHTMLComment(v) {
   212	                                        _, _ = w.WriteString("<!-- raw HTML omitted -->\n")
   213	                                }
   214	                        }
   215	                }
   216	        }
   217	        return ast.WalkContinue, nil
   218	}
   219	
   220	func (r *hugoContextRenderer) renderRawHTML(
   221	        w util.BufWriter, source []byte, node ast.Node, entering bool,
   222	) (ast.WalkStatus, error) {
   223	        if !entering {
   224	                return ast.WalkSkipChildren, nil
   225	        }
   226	        n := node.(*ast.RawHTML)
   227	        l := n.Segments.Len()
   228	        if r.Unsafe {
   229	                for i := range l {
   230	                        segment := n.Segments.At(i)
   231	                        _, _ = w.Write(segment.Value(source))
   232	                }
   233	                return ast.WalkSkipChildren, nil
   234	        }
   235	        segment := n.Segments.At(0)
   236	        v := segment.Value(source)
   237	        if !r.isHTMLComment(v) {
   238	                r.logRawHTMLEmittedWarn(w)
   239	                _, _ = w.WriteString("<!-- raw HTML omitted -->")
   240	        }
   241	        return ast.WalkSkipChildren, nil
   242	}
   243	
   244	func (r *hugoContextRenderer) handleHugoContext(w util.BufWriter, source []byte, node ast.Node, entering bool) (ast.WalkStatus, error) {
   245	        if !entering {
   246	                return ast.WalkContinue, nil
   247	        }
   248	
   249	        hctx := node.(*HugoContext)
   250	        ctx, ok := w.(*render.Context)
   251	        if !ok {
   252	                return ast.WalkContinue, nil
   253	        }
   254	        if hctx.Closing {
   255	                _ = ctx.PopPid()
   256	        } else {
   257	                ctx.PushPid(hctx.Pid)
   258	        }
   259	        return ast.WalkContinue, nil
   260	}
   261	
   262	type hugoContextTransformer struct{}
   263	
   264	var _ parser.ASTTransformer = (*hugoContextTransformer)(nil)
   265	
   266	func (a *hugoContextTransformer) Transform(n *ast.Document, reader text.Reader, pc parser.Context) {
   267	        ast.Walk(n, func(n ast.Node, entering bool) (ast.WalkStatus, error) {
   268	                s := ast.WalkContinue
   269	                if !entering || n.Kind() != kindHugoContext {
   270	                        return s, nil
   271	                }
   272	
   273	                if p, ok := n.Parent().(*ast.Paragraph); ok {
   274	                        if p.ChildCount() == 1 {
   275	                                // Avoid empty paragraphs.
   276	                                p.Parent().ReplaceChild(p.Parent(), p, n)
   277	                        } else {
   278	                                if t, ok := n.PreviousSibling().(*ast.Text); ok {
   279	                                        // Remove the newline produced by the Hugo context markers.
   280	                                        if t.SoftLineBreak() {
   281	                                                if t.Segment.Len() == 0 {
   282	                                                        p.RemoveChild(p, t)
   283	                                                } else {
   284	                                                        t.SetSoftLineBreak(false)
   285	                                                }
   286	                                        }
   287	                                }
   288	                        }
   289	                }
   290	
   291	                return s, nil
   292	        })
   293	}
   294	
   295	type hugoContextExtension struct {
   296	        logger loggers.Logger
   297	}
   298	
   299	func (a *hugoContextExtension) Extend(m goldmark.Markdown) {
   300	        m.Parser().AddOptions(
   301	                parser.WithInlineParsers(
   302	                        util.Prioritized(&hugoContextParser{}, 50),
   303	                ),
   304	                parser.WithASTTransformers(util.Prioritized(&hugoContextTransformer{}, 10)),
   305	        )
   306	
   307	        m.Renderer().AddOptions(
   308	                renderer.WithNodeRenderers(
   309	                        util.Prioritized(&hugoContextRenderer{
   310	                                logger: a.logger,
   311	                                Config: html.Config{
   312	                                        Writer: html.DefaultWriter,
   313	                                },
   314	                        }, 50),
   315	                ),
   316	        )
   317	}

   254	func (sc shortcode) String() string {
   255	        // for testing (mostly), so any change here will break tests!
   256	        var params any
   257	        switch v := sc.params.(type) {
   258	        case map[string]any:
   259	                // sort the keys so test assertions won't fail
   260	                var keys []string
   261	                for k := range v {
   262	                        keys = append(keys, k)
   263	                }
   264	                sort.Strings(keys)
   265	                tmp := make(map[string]any)
   266	
   267	                for _, k := range keys {
   268	                        tmp[k] = v[k]
   269	                }
   270	                params = tmp
   271	
   272	        default:
   273	                // use it as is
   274	                params = sc.params
   275	        }
   276	
   277	        return fmt.Sprintf("%s(%q, %t){%s}", sc.name, params, sc.doMarkup, sc.inner)
   278	}
   279	
   280	// shared between all pages from the same source file.
   281	type shortcodeParseInfo struct {
   282	        filename           string
   283	        firstTemplateStore *tplimpl.TemplateStore // This represents the first site and must not be used for execution.
   284	
   285	        // Ordered list of shortcodes.
   286	        shortcodes []*shortcode
   287	
   288	        // All the shortcode names in this set.
   289	        nameSetMu sync.RWMutex
   290	        nameSet   map[string]bool
   291	
   292	        // Configuration
   293	        enableInlineShortcodes bool
   294	}
   295	
   296	func (s *shortcodeParseInfo) addName(name string) {
   297	        s.nameSetMu.Lock()
   298	        defer s.nameSetMu.Unlock()
   299	        s.nameSet[name] = true
   300	}
   301	
   302	func (s *shortcodeParseInfo) hasName(name string) bool {
   303	        s.nameSetMu.RLock()
   304	        defer s.nameSetMu.RUnlock()
   305	        _, ok := s.nameSet[name]
   306	        return ok
   307	}
   308	
   309	func newShortcodeHandler(filename string, d *deps.Deps) *shortcodeParseInfo {
   310	        sh := &shortcodeParseInfo{
   311	                filename:               filename,
   312	                firstTemplateStore:     d.TemplateStore,
   313	                enableInlineShortcodes: d.ExecHelper.Sec().EnableInlineShortcodes,
   314	                shortcodes:             make([]*shortcode, 0, 4),
   315	                nameSet:                make(map[string]bool),
   316	        }
   317	
   318	        return sh
   319	}

   322	        innerNewlineRegexp = "\n"
   323	        innerCleanupRegexp = `\A<p>(.*)</p>\n\z`
   324	        innerCleanupExpand = "$1"
   325	)
   326	
   327	func prepareShortcode(
   328	        level int,
   329	        sc *shortcode,
   330	        parent *ShortcodeWithPage,
   331	        po *pageOutput,
   332	        isRenderString bool,
   333	) (shortcodeRenderer, error) {
   334	        p := po.p
   335	        toParseErr := func(err error) error {
   336	                source := p.m.content.mustSource()
   337	                return p.parseError(fmt.Errorf("failed to render shortcode %q: %w", sc.name, err), source, sc.pos)
   338	        }
   339	
   340	        // Allow the caller to delay the rendering of the shortcode if needed.
   341	        var fn shortcodeRenderFunc = func(ctx context.Context) ([]byte, bool, error) {
   342	                if p.m.pageConfigSource.ContentMediaType.IsMarkdown() && sc.doMarkup {
   343	                        // Signal downwards that the content rendered will be
   344	                        // parsed and rendered by Goldmark.
   345	                        ctx = tpl.Context.IsInGoldmark.Set(ctx, true)
   346	                }
   347	                r, err := doRenderShortcode(ctx, level, po.p.s.TemplateStore, sc, parent, po, isRenderString)
   348	                if err != nil {
   349	                        return nil, false, toParseErr(err)
   350	                }
   351	
   352	                b, hasVariants, err := r.renderShortcode(ctx)
   353	                if err != nil {
   354	                        return nil, false, toParseErr(err)
   355	                }
   356	                return b, hasVariants, nil
   357	        }
   358	
   359	        return fn, nil
   360	}
   361

   372	        p := po.p
   373	
   374	        // Tracks whether this shortcode or any of its children has template variations
   375	        // in other languages or output formats. We are currently only interested in
   376	        // the output formats.
   377	        var hasVariants bool
   378	
   379	        if sc.isInline {
   380	                if !p.s.ExecHelper.Sec().EnableInlineShortcodes {
   381	                        return zeroShortcode, nil
   382	                }
   383	                templatePath := path.Join("_inline_shortcode", p.Path(), sc.name)
   384	                if sc.isClosing {
   385	                        templStr := sc.innerString()
   386	
   387	                        var err error
   388	                        tmpl, err = ts.TextParse(templatePath, templStr)
   389	                        if err != nil {
   390	                                if isRenderString {

   180	        itemsStep2 []any
   181	
   182	        // The shortcode handler.
   183	        shortcodeParseInfo *shortcodeParseInfo

   185	
   186	func (pi *contentParseInfo) AddBytes(item pageparser.Item) {
   187	        pi.itemsStep2 = append(pi.itemsStep2, item)
   188	}
   189	
   190	func (pi *contentParseInfo) AddReplacement(val []byte, source pageparser.Item) {
   191	        pi.itemsStep2 = append(pi.itemsStep2, pageContentReplacement{val: val, source: source})
   192	}
   193	
   194	func (pi *contentParseInfo) AddShortcode(s *shortcode) {
   195	        pi.itemsStep2 = append(pi.itemsStep2, s)
   196	        if s.insertPlaceholder() {
   197	                pi.hasNonMarkdownShortcode = true
   198	        }
   199	}
   200	
   201	// sourceMapEntry maps a range in rendered content back to a position in the original source.
   202	type sourceMapEntry struct {
   203	        renderOffset int  // start offset in content sent to Goldmark
   204	        sourceOffset int  // corresponding offset in original source file
   205	        isShortcode  bool // if true, any pos in this segment maps to sourceOffset
   206	}
   207	
   208	// resolveSourceOffset maps a position in rendered content to an offset in the original source.
   209	func resolveSourceOffset(sm []sourceMapEntry, pos int) int {
   210	        i := sort.Search(len(sm), func(i int) bool {
   211	                return sm[i].renderOffset > pos
   212	        }) - 1
   213	        if i < 0 {
   214	                return pos
   215	        }
   216	        e := sm[i]
   217	        if e.isShortcode {
   218	                return e.sourceOffset
   219	        }
   220	        return e.sourceOffset + (pos - e.renderOffset)
   221	}
   222	
   223	// contentToRenderForItems returns the content to be processed by Goldmark or similar.
   224	func (pi *contentParseInfo) contentToRender(ctx context.Context, source []byte, renderedShortcodes map[string]shortcodeRenderer) ([]byte, []sourceMapEntry, bool, error) {
   225	        var hasVariants bool
   226	        c := make([]byte, 0, len(source)+(len(source)/10))
   227	        var sm []sourceMapEntry
   228	
   229	        for _, it := range pi.itemsStep2 {
   230	                switch v := it.(type) {
   231	                case pageparser.Item:
   232	                        sm = append(sm, sourceMapEntry{renderOffset: len(c), sourceOffset: v.Pos()})
   233	                        c = append(c, source[v.Pos():v.Pos()+len(v.Val(source))]...)
   234	                case pageContentReplacement:
   235	                        sm = append(sm, sourceMapEntry{renderOffset: len(c), sourceOffset: v.source.Pos()})
   236	                        c = append(c, v.val...)
   237	                case *shortcode:
   238	                        sm = append(sm, sourceMapEntry{renderOffset: len(c), sourceOffset: v.pos, isShortcode: true})
   239	                        if !v.insertPlaceholder() {
   240	                                // Insert the rendered shortcode.
   241	                                renderedShortcode, found := renderedShortcodes[v.placeholder]
   242	                                if !found {
   243	                                        // This should never happen.
   244	                                        panic(fmt.Sprintf("rendered shortcode %q not found", v.placeholder))
   245	                                }
   246	
   247	                                b, more, err := renderedShortcode.renderShortcode(ctx)
   248	                                if err != nil {
   249	                                        return nil, nil, false, fmt.Errorf("failed to render shortcode: %w", err)
   250	                                }
   251	                                hasVariants = hasVariants || more
   252	                                c = append(c, []byte(b)...)
   253	
   254	                        } else {
   255	                                // Insert the placeholder so we can insert the content after
   256	                                // markdown processing.
   257	                                c = append(c, []byte(v.placeholder)...)
   258	                        }
   259	                default:
   260	                        panic(fmt.Sprintf("unknown item type %T", it))

   267	func (c *cachedContent) IsZero() bool {
   268	        return len(c.pi.itemsStep2) == 0
   269	}
   270	
   271	func (pi *contentParseInfo) parseSource(source []byte, skipFrontMatter bool) error {
   272	        if len(pi.itemsStep1) == 0 {
   273	                return nil
   274	        }
   275	
   276	        s := pi.shortcodeParseInfo
   277	
   278	        fail := func(err error, i pageparser.Item) error {
   279	                if fe, ok := err.(herrors.FileError); ok {
   280	                        return fe
   281	                }
   282	
   283	                pos := posFromInput("", source, i.Pos())
   284	
   285	                return herrors.NewFileErrorFromPos(err, pos)
   286	        }
   287	
   288	        iter := pageparser.NewIterator(pi.itemsStep1)
   289	
   290	        // the parser is guaranteed to return items in proper order or fail, so …
   291	        // … it's safe to keep some "global" state
   292	        var ordinal int
   293	
   294	Loop:
   295	        for {
   296	                it := iter.Next()
   297	
   298	                switch {
   299	                case it.Type == pageparser.TypeIgnore:
   300	                case it.IsFrontMatter():
   301	                        if !skipFrontMatter {
   302	                                if err := pi.parseFrontMatter(it, iter, source); err != nil {
   303	                                        return err
   304	                                }
   305	                        }
   306	                        next := iter.Peek()
   307	                        if !next.IsDone() {
   308	                                pi.posMainContent = next.Pos()
   309	                        }
   310	                case it.Type == pageparser.TypeLeadSummaryDivider:
   311	                        posBody := -1
   312	                        f := func(item pageparser.Item) bool {
   313	                                if posBody == -1 && !item.IsDone() {
   314	                                        posBody = item.Pos()
   315	                                }
   316	
   317	                                if item.IsNonWhitespace(source) {
   318	                                        // Done
   319	                                        return false
   320	                                }
   321	                                return true
   322	                        }
   323	                        iter.PeekWalk(f)
   324	
   325	                        pi.hasSummaryDivider = true
   326	
   327	                        // The content may be rendered by Goldmark or similar,
   328	                        // and we need to track the summary.
   329	                        pi.AddReplacement(internalSummaryDividerPre, it)
   330

    30	        renderShortcode(context.Context) ([]byte, bool, error)
    31	        renderShortcodeString(context.Context) (string, bool, error)

    38	}
    39	
    40	func (f shortcodeRenderFunc) renderShortcodeString(ctx context.Context) (string, bool, error) {
    41	        b, has, err := f(ctx)
    42	        return string(b), has, err
    43	}

    48	}

    51	        return []byte(p.s), p.hasVariants, nil
    52	}
    53	
    54	func (p prerenderedShortcode) renderShortcodeString(context.Context) (string, bool, error) {

    56	}

   541	func (s *shortcodeParseInfo) prepareShortcodesForPage(po *pageOutput, isRenderString bool) (map[string]shortcodeRenderer, error) {
   542	        rendered := make(map[string]shortcodeRenderer)
   543	
   544	        for _, v := range s.shortcodes {

   546	                if err != nil {

   550	        }

   553	}

   555	func posFromInput(filename string, input []byte, offset int) text.Position {
   556	        if offset < 0 || offset > len(input) {
   557	                return text.Position{
   558	                        Filename: filename,
   559	                }
   560	        }
   561	        lf := []byte("\n")
   562	        input = input[:offset]
   563	        lineNumber := bytes.Count(input, lf) + 1
   564	        endOfLastLine := bytes.LastIndex(input, lf)
   565	
   566	        return text.Position{
   567	                Filename:     filename,
   568	                LineNumber:   lineNumber,
   569	                ColumnNumber: offset - endOfLastLine,
   570	                Offset:       offset,
   571	        }
   572	}
   573	
   574	// pageTokens state:
   575	// - before: positioned just before the shortcode start
   576	// - after: shortcode(s) consumed (plural when they are nested)
   577	func (s *shortcodeParseInfo) extractShortcode(ordinal, level int, source []byte, pt *pageparser.Iterator) (*shortcode, error) {
   578	        if s == nil {
   579	                panic("handler nil")
   580	        }
   581	        sc := &shortcode{ordinal: ordinal}
   582	
   583	        // Back up one to identify any indentation.
   584	        if pt.Pos() > 0 {
   585	                pt.Backup()
   586	                item := pt.Next()
   587	                if item.IsIndentation() {
   588	                        sc.indentation = item.ValStr(source)
   589	                }
   590	        }
